Sun Microsystems attracted world-class talent by giving away equity instead of hoarding it. The founders kept less than half, early hires received a comparable or larger share, and about 40% went to investors after Series A. This approach helped bring in world-class engineers and future leaders, including co-founders Andy Bechtolsheim and Bill Joy, as well as Eric Schmidt. By using ownership as an incentive, Sun built a team that was deeply invested in both the companyвҖҷs growth and its future. Follow us (@entrepreneursonig) for everything related to entrepreneurs. рҹҳ… (via @danmancarney) Grand Theft Auto is a long-running and influential video game series developed by Rockstar Games. First launched in 1997, the series is known for its open-world design, giving players the freedom to explore vast urban environments, engage in missions, and interact with a wide range of characters. The core gameplay often revolves around criminal activity, including car theft, heists, and gang conflicts, but the real draw is the freedom it offersвҖ”players can follow the storyline or simply roam the world causing chaos, completing side missions, or just exploring. Each major title in the series has raised the bar in terms of scale, realism, and storytelling. What sets GTA apart is its mix of dark humor, social commentary, and satirical take on modern society. From fictional versions of American cities like Liberty City (New York), Vice City (Miami), and Los Santos (Los Angeles), the games offer not just action but a reflection of real-world issues through exaggerated, often absurd scenarios. Over time, GTA has become a cultural icon, influencing not just gaming but also music, fashion, and even how open-world games are designed. Despite controversies over violence and mature themes, its impact on gaming is undeniable, and it continues to be one of the most successful and talked-about franchises in the industry.

The Prompting Company, a Y Combinator-backed startup, is pioneering a new approach to product discovery through AI tools like ChatGPT. The company specializes in Generative Engine Optimization (GEO), a technique designed to help brands appear in AI-generated recommendations. Rather than traditional SEO, GEO focuses on creating AI-facing websitesвҖ”streamlined pages tailored for AI agents rather than human users. Founded by Kevin Chandra, Michelle Marcelline, and Albert Purnama, all Indonesian immigrants and repeat YC founders, the startup recently secured $6.5 million in seed funding from investors including Peak XV Partners, Base10, and Y Combinator. Their client roster includes notable companies such as Rippling, Rho, Motion, and a Fortune 10 firm. The Prompting Company currently hosts over 500,000 AI-optimized pages, generating millions of monthly visits. Their system identifies purchase-intent queries from AI models, generates structured responses, and routes AI agents to relevant product pages. This strategy is expected to significantly boost AI-driven trafficвҖ”by as much as 520% in 2025 compared to the previous year. Looking ahead, the company is collaborating with Nvidia on next-generation AI search technologies. They envision a future where AI agents not only recommend products but also complete transactions on behalf of users, fundamentally reshaping how e-commerce operates. Source: Tech Crunch

Brian Chesky, cofounder of Airbnb, once read aloud an investorвҖҷs rejection letter вҖ” and the irony is brutal. Back in the early days, Airbnb tried raising just $150,000 at a $1.5M valuation. One investor passed, writing: вҖңThe potential market opportunity did not seem large enough for our model.вҖқ Fast forward to today: Airbnb now processes nearly as much money as the entire GDP of Croatia. Roughly $1 of every $1,500 spent worldwide flows through Airbnb. And the core business model? Almost identical to what they pitched in that rejection email. Reddit, now a global hub with over 1.7 billion monthly visitors, started out with a clever illusion. In its earliest days, founders Alexis Ohanian and Steve Huffman posted nearly all the content themselvesвҖ”using fake usernames to make the platform feel alive. This wasn't deception for deception's sakeвҖ”it was strategy. By simulating a bustling community, they sparked genuine user interest and engagement. It's a powerful reminder that early-stage growth often demands bold, unconventional moves. The lesson? Momentum doesn't always start naturally. Founders must be willing to roll up their sleeves, create the spark, and build value from the ground upвҖ”even if it means faking the crowd before the crowd arrives. рқҷ§рқҷ–рқҷҳрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷң рқҷқрқҷҡрқҷ§рқҷһрқҷ©рқҷ–рқҷңрқҷҡ рқҷҶрқҷҡрқҷ® рқҷӣрқҷҡрқҷ–рқҷ©рқҷӘрқҷ§рқҷҡрқҷЁ рқҷӨрқҷӣ рқҷ§рқҷҡрқҷҳрқҷҡрқҷЈрқҷ© рқҷўрқҷӨрқҷҷрқҷҡрқҷЎрқҷЁ рқҷһрқҷЈрқҷҳрқҷЎрқҷӘрқҷҷрқҷҡ 1. * рқҷҖрқҷЈрқҷңрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷҡ*: рқҳј рқҷ©рқҷӘрқҷ§рқҷ—рқҷӨрқҷҳрқҷқрқҷ–рқҷ§рқҷңрқҷҡрқҷҷ рқҷЎрқҷһрқҷ©рқҷҡрқҷ§ рқҷһрқҷЈрқҷЎрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷҡрқҷӣрқҷӨрқҷӘрқҷ§ рқҷҡрқҷЈрқҷңрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷҡ рқҷ©рқҷ®рқҷҘрқҷһрқҷҳрқҷ–рқҷЎрқҷЎрқҷ® рқҷҘрқҷ§рқҷӨрқҷҷрқҷӘрқҷҳрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷң рқҷ–рқҷ§рқҷӨрқҷӘрқҷЈрқҷҷ рқҷқрқҷӨрқҷ§рқҷЁрқҷҡрқҷҘрқҷӨрқҷ¬рқҷҡрқҷ§ рқҷҷрқҷҡрқҷҘрқҷҡрқҷЈрқҷҷрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷң рқҷӨрқҷЈ рқҷ©рқҷқрқҷҡ рқҷўрқҷӨрқҷҷрқҷҡрқҷЎ рқҷ®рқҷҡрқҷ–рқҷ§ 2.* рқҷҸрқҷ§рқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷЁрқҷўрқҷһрқҷЁрқҷЁрқҷһрқҷӨрқҷЈ*: рқҳј рқҷЁрқҷҘрқҷҡрқҷҡрқҷҷ рқҷўрқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷӘрқҷ–рқҷЎ рқҷ©рқҷ§рқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷЁрқҷўрқҷһрқҷЁрқҷЁрқҷһрқҷӨрқҷЈ рқҷӨрқҷӣрқҷӣрқҷҡрқҷ§рқҷһрқҷЈрқҷң рқҷҘрқҷ§рқҷҡрқҷҳрқҷһрқҷЁрқҷҡ рқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷҷ рқҷҡрқҷЈрқҷңрқҷ–рқҷңрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷң рқҷңрқҷҡрқҷ–рқҷ§ рқҷЁрқҷқрқҷһрқҷӣрқҷ©рқҷЁ 3.* рқҷӢрқҷҡрқҷ§рқҷӣрқҷӨрқҷ§рқҷўрқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷҳрқҷҡ *: рқҷ„рқҷ© рқҷ—рқҷӨрқҷ–рқҷЁрқҷ©рқҷЁ рқҷһрқҷўрқҷҘрқҷ§рқҷҡрқҷЁрқҷЁрқҷһрқҷ«рқҷҡ рқҷ–рқҷҳрқҷҳрқҷҡрқҷЎрқҷҡрқҷ§рқҷ–рқҷ©рқҷһрқҷӨрқҷЈ рқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷҷ рқҷқрқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷҷрқҷЎрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷң рқҷ¬рқҷһрқҷ©рқҷқ рқҷ– рқҷӣрқҷӨрқҷҳрқҷӘрқҷЁ рқҷӨрқҷЈ рқҷ–рқҷңрқҷһрқҷЎрқҷһрқҷ©рқҷ® рқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷҷ рқҷҷрқҷ§рқҷһрқҷ«рқҷһрқҷЈрқҷң рқҷҷрқҷ®рқҷЈрқҷ–рқҷўрқҷһрқҷҳрқҷЁ 4.* рқҳҝрқҷҡрқҷЁрқҷһрқҷңрқҷЈ*: рқҳҝрқҷһрқҷЁрқҷ©рқҷһрқҷЈрқҷҳрқҷ©рқҷһрқҷ«рқҷҡ рқҷЁрқҷ©рқҷ®рқҷЎрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷң рқҷҡрқҷЎрқҷҡрқҷўрқҷҡрқҷЈрқҷ©рқҷЁ рқҷЎрқҷһрқҷ рқҷҡ рқҷ–рқҷңрқҷңрқҷ§рқҷҡрқҷЁрқҷЁрқҷһрқҷ«рқҷҡ рқҷӣрқҷ§рқҷӨрқҷЈрқҷ© рқҷ—рқҷӘрқҷўрқҷҘрқҷҡрқҷ§рқҷЁ рқҷ§рқҷҡрқҷ–рқҷ§ рқҷЁрқҷҘрқҷӨрқҷһрқҷЎрқҷҡрқҷ§рқҷЁ рқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷҷ рқҷӘрқҷЈрқҷһрқҷҰрқҷӘрқҷҡ рқҷ¬рқҷқрқҷҡрқҷҡрқҷЎ рқҷҷрқҷҡрқҷЁрқҷһрқҷңрқҷЈрқҷЁ 5. вҒ *рқҷ„рқҷЈрқҷ©рқҷҡрқҷ§рқҷһрқҷӨрқҷ§*: рқҷҚрқҷ–рқҷҳрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷңрқҷһрқҷЈрқҷЁрқҷҘрқҷһрқҷ§рқҷҡрқҷҷ рқҷ¬рқҷһрқҷ©рқҷқ рқҷЁрқҷӘрқҷҘрқҷҘрқҷӨрқҷ§рқҷ©рқҷһрқҷ«рқҷҡ рқҷЁрқҷҡрқҷ–рқҷ©рқҷЁ рқҷ– рқҷҷрқҷ§рқҷһрқҷ«рқҷҡрқҷ§рқҷӣрқҷӨрқҷҳрқҷӘрқҷЁрқҷҡрқҷҷ рқҷҳрқҷӨрқҷҳрқҷ рқҷҘрқҷһрқҷ© рқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷҷ рқҷ–рқҷҷрқҷ«рқҷ–рқҷЈрқҷҳрқҷҡрқҷҷ рқҷ©рқҷҡрқҷҳрқҷқрқҷЈрқҷӨрқҷЎрқҷӨрқҷңрқҷ® Successful founders are idea machines. Sam Altman once shared how Y Combinator funded 20 talented teams who had everything except an idea. The result? All of them failed. Why? Because having ideas isnвҖҷt a one-time thingвҖ”itвҖҷs a skill you need to practice regularly. Altman explained, вҖңYou have to come up with crazy new ideas and big changes all the time.вҖқ That means seeing problems differently, thinking creatively, and imagining solutions that donвҖҷt exist yet but should. Think of it this way: a founderвҖҷs job doesnвҖҷt end with launching a company. ItвҖҷs about staying curious, asking questions, and continuously innovating. The ability to adapt, refine, and dream up new possibilities is what separates good founders from great ones. So, if you want to lead something extraordinary, donвҖҷt stop at one idea. Keep the ideas flowingвҖ”thatвҖҷs how you build something that lasts. Media: Y Combinator (2018)

COMMENT вҖҳCARвҖҷ FOR PROJECT FILES рҹҡҖ This is my first time trying out 3D Car Animation in Blender. The University Grants Commission (UGC) has approved a proposal allowing Indian universities and higher education institutions to conduct admissions twice a year, similar to many foreign universities. Starting from the 2024-25 academic session, Indian universities will be able to enroll students during two distinct cycles, one in July-August and another in January-February, UGC chief Jagadesh Kumar announced. This change is aimed at benefiting students who might miss the opportunity to enroll during the traditional admission period due to delays in board exam results, health issues, or other personal circumstances. He also noted that this new system would facilitate campus recruitment opportunities twice a year, potentially enhancing job prospects for graduates. Moreover, biannual admissions could help universities manage their resourcesвҖ”such as faculty, laboratories, classrooms, and support servicesвҖ”more effectively, improving operational efficiency. Kumar highlighted that adopting a biannual admission process would bring Indian institutions in line with global standards, enhancing their international appeal and facilitating more extensive collaborations and student exchanges. He emphasized that while the move to biannual admissions offers significant advantages, it requires careful planning and adjustment of administrative processes to ensure resources are optimally utilized and support systems are robust enough to handle students entering at different times of the year. However, Kumar clarified that implementing biannual admissions would not be compulsory for all institutions. "Only those universities and higher education institutions that have the necessary infrastructure and faculty are encouraged to adopt this system. It is an opportunity for those institutions willing to expand their student base and introduce new programs in emerging fields," he added. Institutions interested in this system will need to make appropriate amendments to their regulations to facilitate admissions in two cycles each year. Facing challenges like dwindling audiences and fewer movie releases, cinemas across India are gearing up to offer discounted tickets to attract more moviegoers. On May 31 (tomorrow), designated as Cinema Lovers Day, major multiplex chains and single-screen cinemas will offer tickets at a reduced price of Rs 99. This initiative, endorsed by prominent chains such as PVR Inox, Cinepolis India, Miraj Cinemas, Multa A2, and MovieMax, aims to revitalize the theatre-going experience. Kamal Gianchandani, the CEO of PVR Inox Pictures and head of the Multiplex Association of India (MAI), shared that this initiative will cover approximately 4,000 screens across the country. Although premium seating like recliners will not be included, about 90-95% of the seats will be available at this discounted rate. In addition to multiplexes, many single-screen theatres, especially in the southern regions of India, are participating, with some offering tickets for even less than Rs 99, possibly down to Rs 70. Gianchandani emphasized that while the discount is limited to just one day, it is expected to provide a significant boost to the box office as the summer holiday season begins. He noted that the cinema industry is preparing for a busy season with several film releases lined up, following a quieter period in April and May due to the elections. "The supply of movies will change dramatically compared to the last two to three months. Starting June, we are expecting a lot of clashes as many producers held back their releases," Gianchandani explained. Highlighting the broader impact of such promotional days, Gianchandani pointed out that initiatives like these make movie-going more accessible for families and students, especially during the peak summer season when schools are on break. Reflecting on the success of similar past initiatives, such as National Cinema Day in 2022 which saw ticket sales exceed 6.5 million, Gianchandani is optimistic about the potential impact of Cinema Lovers Day. . . . #TheTatva #TatvaNews #India #Cinema #Movie #Theatre #Lover #Ticket #Money #Discount #Sale #Mall #Multiplex #Film #Actor #Actress #Audience

Mark Zuckerberg emphasizes the misconception surrounding the process of idea formation, debunking the notion of a single eureka moment as a fallacy perpetuated by movies and pop culture. He shares a secret: nobody possesses all the knowledge or skills necessary to execute a grand idea from the outset. Instead, ideas evolve and become clearer through active engagement and work. Zuckerberg underscores the importance of taking the first step, highlighting that if he had waited until he knew everything about connecting people, Facebook would never have been created. He encourages aspiring entrepreneurs not to be discouraged by their perceived lack of a eureka moment but to instead recognize that ideas develop over time and with effort. By demystifying the creative process, Zuckerberg empowers individuals to overcome their fear of inadequacy and hesitation, urging them to embrace the journey of exploration and innovation.
